	//Summary: Returns the absolute URL to use for prefixing any Ajax URL call.
	//Returns: The absolute URL to use for prefixing any Ajax URL call.
	function getAbsoluteURL() {
		if (absoluteURL != "") {
			var currentURL = document.URL;
			var currentProtocol = "";

			if (currentURL.indexOf("://") != -1) {
				currentProtocol = currentURL.substring(0, currentURL
						.indexOf("://"));
			}

			var savedProtocol = "";
			if (absoluteURL.indexOf("://") != -1) {
				savedProtocol = absoluteURL.substring(0, absoluteURL
						.indexOf("://"));
			}

			if (currentProtocol != savedProtocol) {
				absoluteURL = currentProtocol
						+ absoluteURL.substring(absoluteURL.indexOf("://"));
			}
		}

		return absoluteURL;
	}
	function getAbsoluteBaseURL() {
		if (absoluteBaseURL != "") {
			var currentURL = document.URL;
			var currentProtocol = "";

			if (currentURL.indexOf("://") != -1) {
				currentProtocol = currentURL.substring(0, currentURL
						.indexOf("://"));
			}

			var savedProtocol = "";
			if (absoluteBaseURL.indexOf("://") != -1) {
				savedProtocol = absoluteBaseURL.substring(0, absoluteURL
						.indexOf("://"));
			}

			if (currentProtocol != savedProtocol) {
				absoluteBaseURL = currentProtocol
						+ absoluteBaseURL.substring(absoluteBaseURL
								.indexOf("://"));
			}
		}

		return absoluteBaseURL;
	}

					<script>

$(document).ready(function() {
	cookieSetUp();
});

$(document).on("click", "#CybotCookiebotDialogBodyLevelButtonLevelOptinAllowAll", function(){
    cookieSetUp();
});

$(document).on("click", "#CybotCookiebotDialogBodyLevelButtonLevelOptinAllowallSelection", function(){
    cookieSetUp();
});

function cookieSetUp(){
/* linkwise-footer-content */


	const url = window.location.href;
	const expiryDays = 30;

	let paidUrlType, lkws_138ID, affiliateCookie;
	let cookieConsent = $("#cookiebanner").length;
	let paidSession = sessionStorage.getItem('paidSession');
	let referrer = document.referrer;

	console.log('version 1.4');

	if (url.indexOf('lkws_138') > 0 || referrer.indexOf('lkws_138') > 0) {
		if (url.indexOf('adhocPriceActive=true') < 0 && referrer.indexOf('adhocPriceActive=true') < 0){
			lkws_138ID = getParameterByName ('lkws_138', url);
			if (lkws_138ID == null) {
				lkws_138ID = getParameterByName ('lkws_138', referrer);
			}
			paidUrlType = lkws_138ID;
			sessionStorage.setItem('paidSession', paidUrlType);
			paidSession = sessionStorage.getItem('paidSession');		
		}
		else if (url.indexOf('adhocPriceActive=true') > 0 || referrer.indexOf('adhocPriceActive=true') > 0) {
			paidUrlType = "cookiePricePaidLastReferral";
			sessionStorage.setItem('paidSession', paidUrlType);
			paidSession = sessionStorage.getItem('paidSession');
		
		} 
		
	} else if (url.indexOf('fbclid') > 0 || referrer.indexOf('fbclid') > 0) {
		paidUrlType = "fbPaidLastReferral";
		sessionStorage.setItem('paidSession', paidUrlType);
		paidSession = sessionStorage.getItem('paidSession');

	} else if (url.indexOf('gclid') > 0 || referrer.indexOf('gclid') > 0) {
		paidUrlType = "gPaidLastReferral";
		sessionStorage.setItem('paidSession', paidUrlType);
		paidSession = sessionStorage.getItem('paidSession');
		
	}  else if (url.indexOf('cmicc=skroutz') > 0 || referrer.indexOf('cmicc=skroutz') > 0) {
		paidUrlType = "skroutzPaidLastReferral";
		sessionStorage.setItem('paidSession', paidUrlType);
		paidSession = sessionStorage.getItem('paidSession');
		
	}   else if (url.indexOf('bpgid:') > 0 || referrer.indexOf('bpgid:') > 0) {
		paidUrlType = "bestPricePaidLastReferral";
		sessionStorage.setItem('paidSession', paidUrlType);
		paidSession = sessionStorage.getItem('paidSession');
		
	} else if (url.indexOf('adhocPriceActive=true') > 0 || referrer.indexOf('adhocPriceActive=true') > 0) {
		paidUrlType = "cookiePricePaidLastReferral";
		sessionStorage.setItem('paidSession', paidUrlType);
		paidSession = sessionStorage.getItem('paidSession');
		
	} 
	

	if (paidUrlType !== undefined && paidSession !== undefined) {
		sessionStorage.removeItem('paidSession');
		sessionStorage.setItem('paidSession', paidUrlType);
		
	}	
		
	
	setTimeout(function() {
		if (paidSession !== null && getCookie("CookieConsent")!== '' && getCookie("CookieConsent")!== null) {
			switch (paidUrlType) {
				case lkws_138ID:
					if (lkws_138ID !== undefined) {
						setCookie("lkws_138", lkws_138ID, expiryDays);	
					}else {
						setCookie("lkws_138", paidSession, expiryDays);	
					}						
					break;
				case "fbPaidLastReferral":
					affiliateCookie = getCookie("lkws_138");
					if (affiliateCookie !== '' && affiliateCookie !== null) {
						setCookie("lkws_138", "fbPaidLastReferral");					
					}
					break;
				case "gPaidLastReferral":
					affiliateCookie = getCookie("lkws_138");
					if (affiliateCookie !== '' && affiliateCookie !== null) {
						setCookie("lkws_138", "gPaidLastReferral");					
					}
					break;
				case "skroutzPaidLastReferral":
					affiliateCookie = getCookie("lkws_138");
					if (affiliateCookie !== '' && affiliateCookie !== null) {
						setCookie("lkws_138", "skroutzPaidLastReferral");					
					}
					break;
				case "bestPricePaidLastReferral":
					affiliateCookie = getCookie("lkws_138");
					if (affiliateCookie !== '' && affiliateCookie !== null) {
						setCookie("lkws_138", "bestPricePaidLastReferral");					
					}
					break;
				case "cookiePricePaidLastReferral":
					affiliateCookie = getCookie("lkws_138");
					if (affiliateCookie !== '' && affiliateCookie !== null) {
						setCookie("lkws_138", "cookiePricePaidLastReferral");					
					}
			}			
		}
	}, 2000);	
}
	function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
		var d = new Date();
		d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
		var expires = "expires=" + d.toGMTString();
		document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
	}
	function getCookie(cname) {
		var name = cname + "=";
		var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
		var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
		for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
			var c = ca[i];
			while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
				c = c.substring(1);
			}
			if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
				return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
			}
		}
		return "";
	}
	function getParameterByName(name, url) {
		name = name.replace(/[\[\]]/g, '\\$&');
		var regex = new RegExp('[?&]' + name + '(=([^&#]*)|&|#|$)'),
			results = regex.exec(url);
		if (!results) return null;
		if (!results[2]) return '';
		return decodeURIComponent(results[2].replace(/\+/g, ' '));
	}
</script>

		console.log("date8: ",str);
		// Check if we are in Basket Page and if we have a certain Date to Hide 24h Delivery
		if ((day == 25 && month == 12 && year == 2022) || (day == 26 && month == 12 && year == 2022) || (day == 1 && month == 1 && year == 2023) || (day == 2 && month == 1 && year == 2023) || (day == 6 && month == 1 && year == 2023)) {
			$(".Kotsovolos footer").append("<style>.Kotsovolos #delivery24h, .Kotsovolos [expressavailabilityhomeforbigbox], .Kotsovolos [expressavailabilityhome] { display: none !important; }</style>");	
			$('.Kotsovolos #delivery24h').hide();	
			$('.Kotsovolos [expressavailabilityhomeforbigbox]').hide();	
			$('.Kotsovolos [expressavailabilityhome]').hide();	
			console.log(str);		
		}
	}) 
	</script>

	//Summary: Returns the absolute URL to use for prefixing any Ajax URL call.
	//Returns: The absolute URL to use for prefixing any Ajax URL call.
	function getAbsoluteURL() {
		if (absoluteURL != "") {
			var currentURL = document.URL;
			var currentProtocol = "";

			if (currentURL.indexOf("://") != -1) {
				currentProtocol = currentURL.substring(0, currentURL
						.indexOf("://"));
			}

			var savedProtocol = "";
			if (absoluteURL.indexOf("://") != -1) {
				savedProtocol = absoluteURL.substring(0, absoluteURL
						.indexOf("://"));
			}

			if (currentProtocol != savedProtocol) {
				absoluteURL = currentProtocol
						+ absoluteURL.substring(absoluteURL.indexOf("://"));
			}
		}

		return absoluteURL;
	}
	function getAbsoluteBaseURL() {
		if (absoluteBaseURL != "") {
			var currentURL = document.URL;
			var currentProtocol = "";

			if (currentURL.indexOf("://") != -1) {
				currentProtocol = currentURL.substring(0, currentURL
						.indexOf("://"));
			}

			var savedProtocol = "";
			if (absoluteBaseURL.indexOf("://") != -1) {
				savedProtocol = absoluteBaseURL.substring(0, absoluteURL
						.indexOf("://"));
			}

			if (currentProtocol != savedProtocol) {
				absoluteBaseURL = currentProtocol
						+ absoluteBaseURL.substring(absoluteBaseURL
								.indexOf("://"));
			}
		}

		return absoluteBaseURL;
	}
